    ORDER BY (SELECT 1)
    OFFSET @__p_0 ROWS FETCH NEXT @__p_1 ROWS ONLY
) AS [i0]

    SELECT [i1].[Id], [i1].[ConversionRate], [i1].[IsBaseUnit], [i1].[ItemId], [i1].[Price], [i1].[UnitId], [u].[Id] AS [Id0], [u].[NameAr], [u].[NameEn], [u].[ShortName]
    FROM [ItemUnits] AS [i1]
    INNER JOIN [Units] AS [u] ON [i1].[UnitId] = [u].[Id]
) AS [s0] ON [i0].[Id] = [s0].[ItemId]
ORDER BY [i0].[Id], [s].[Id], [c].[Id], [s0].[Id]
